name:Lâ€iâ€uâ€wâ€uâ€sâ€hâ€uâ€aâ€nâ€g
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted April 13, 2024
msg:Accompanying my husband to drive back to Shanghai to visit the graves, we traveled along the way. The first stop was Meizhou. Considering the comprehensive factors such as grade, geographical location, and evaluation, we chose Meizhou Yingbin Hotel on Ctrip. Didn't pay attention to the star rating of the hotel? Judging from the overall grade of decoration and basic services, it is probably a quasi-4-star hotel. The decoration materials and quality are relatively good. The style is traditional. The lobby is magnificent, with many jade sculptures and high-end mahogany furniture; the room is in good sanitary condition, clean and tidy, and the bathroom is large. The service is also good. The waiters are all smiling, answering questions, and free parking. According to the reviews, the hotel's buffet breakfast is very good. It may be because there are few people in the off-season. The breakfast variety for the two days we stayed was not much, but it was quite good compared to the accommodation fee. By the way, we tried Sanjidi soup and Meizhou pickled noodles. Therefore, the two days we stayed here were generally comfortable. From the accommodation fee of several tourist spots we chose from Guangzhou to Shanghai by self-driving this time, it may be the hotel with the highest cost performance. The downside is that the room only comes with disposable cotton slippers, not plastic slippers, which is a bit strange. I had to shower barefoot, which was a bit unusual. Also, there were no standard small items such as cotton swabs (luckily I brought my own cotton swabs). Although these items are optional, they are indispensable for a 4-star hotel, which is also a manifestation of inattentive service. Therefore, I feel that the hotel's hardware facilities can reach 4 stars, but it is not 4 stars.

info:Friends
info:6 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted January 27, 2023
msg:Facilities: The hardware is first-class, but the software needs to be improved.
I saw this room on Ctrip and it happened to be two families traveling together, so I thought this would be a good choice. The actual facilities upon entering are not much different from the pictures online. There are tall living rooms, comfortable rooms, and matching mahjong rooms.
Advantages: 1. The room facilities are high-end, the bedding and other items are very comfortable, the mattress is moderately soft and hard, and the pillows and quilts are particularly comfortable.
2. The living room is very comfortable, tall and elegant, and it is comfortable for several families to make tea together.
3. The hotel has a high-end a**osphere, a good location, and convenient parking and transportation.

Disadvantages: 1. The service needs to be improved. Maybe there are few staff during the Spring Festival holiday. I called several times for the required service but there was no response. Later I went to the front desk to call the manager, and the manager himself came up to the floor to solve the problem.
2. There werenâ€™t enough quilts. Even if I asked for an extra bed, I was told there were no quilts. Itâ€™s unimaginable in a five-star hotel.
3. The design of the bathroom is very inhumane. There is no dry and wet separation in the suite. After taking a shower, the whole room is filled with water. The floor is not slippery. The elderly and children are very worried about falling. The hotel room is not equipped with ordinary slippers, so the feet are bare when taking a shower. So cautious
4. There is a lack of mahjong cards, and the hotel service said there is nothing they can do. They should check the facilities every time they check out and clean up. After all, this is also a selling point. Missing cards must be replenished promptly
5. Duplex design. I feel that the renovation of other rooms has not been completed. In addition to the main door, there are three doors that open directly to the corridor. This is a safety hazard. Children can go out after opening it.
6. Breakfast is my biggest complaint. I'm sorry for the price. There are few varieties and the taste is average. The only pickled noodles stall that I think is good has a long queue. When I get to the front of the queue, they say there are no bowls. If the breakfast is usually like this, I'm really sorry for the five-star sign.
